<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Typing in the input and pressing Enter adds new tags</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Clear trigger to remove all tags</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Add tags by pasting into the input</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Delete tags on backspace</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Edit tags after creation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Limit the number of tags</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Navigate tags with keyboard</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Custom validation to accept/reject tags</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the tags input correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the tags input package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> tagsInput</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tags-input&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The tags input package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:tags-input/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" </span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemDeleteTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> value <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> <span class="token entity" title="✕">&amp;#x2715;</span> <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token attr-name">placeholder</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>Add tag...<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>

</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="navigating-and-editing-tags" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Navigating and editing tags<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#navigating-and-editing-tags"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the input has an empty value or the caret is at the start position, the
tags can be selected with the left and right arrow keys. When a tag has visual
focus:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Press <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Enter</code> or double-click the tag to edit it, then press <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Enter</code> to commit
the change.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Pressing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Delete</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Backspace</code> will delete the tag that has &quot;visual&quot; focus.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="setting-the-initial-tags" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial tags<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-tags"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the initial tag values, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property in the machine&#x27;s
context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;React&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Redux&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;TypeScript&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-tags-input" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled tags input<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-tags-input"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To control the tags input programmatically, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code>
properties to the machine function.</p>

<h3 id="controlled-input-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled input value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-input-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">inputValue</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInputValueChange</code> when you need to control the typing
state separately.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  inputValue<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onInputValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setInputValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">inputValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="removing-all-tags" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Removing all tags<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#removing-all-tags"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tags input will remove all tags when the clear button is clicked. To remove
all tags, use the provided <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearTriggerProps</code> function from the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getControlProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getClearTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text"></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To programmatically remove all tags, use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.clearValue()</code>.</p>
<h3 id="usage-within-forms" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within forms<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tags input works when placed within a form and the form is submitted. We
achieve this by:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">ensuring we emit the input event as the value changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">adding a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> attribute to a hidden input so the tags can be
accessed in the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">FormData</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p>To get this feature working you need to pass a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code> option to the context and
render the hidden input with <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getHiddenInputProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;tags&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;React&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Redux&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;TypeScript&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="limiting-the-number-of-tags" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Limiting the number of tags<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#limiting-the-number-of-tags"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To limit the number of tags within the component, you can set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code> property
to the limit you want. The default value is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Infinity</code>.</p>
<p>When the tag reaches the limit, new tags cannot be added except the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow</code> option is passed to the context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">max</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">10</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowOverflow</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="validating-tags" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Validating Tags<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#validating-tags"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Before a tag is added, the machine provides a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">validate</code> function you can use to
determine whether to accept or reject a tag.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Note:</strong> Duplicate tags are prevented by default. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowDuplicates: true</code>
to allow repeatable tags (e.g. sentence builders). Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">validate</code> for custom
rules like format or length.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Common use-cases for validating tags include enforcing format, length, or
content rules.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">validate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// Example: only allow lowercase alphabetic tags</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token regex"><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span><span class="token regex-source language-regex"><span class="token anchor function">^</span><span class="token char-class"><span class="token char-class-punctuation punctuation">[</span><span class="token range">a<span class="token range-punctuation operator">-</span>z</span><span class="token char-class-punctuation punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token quantifier number">+</span><span class="token anchor function">$</span></span><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span></span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">test</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">inputValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allow-duplicates" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allow Duplicates<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allow-duplicates"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, duplicate tags are prevented. For use cases like sentence builders
or repeatable tokens, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowDuplicates: true</code>:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowDuplicates</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="blur-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Blur behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#blur-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tags input is blurred, you can configure the action the machine should
take by passing the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">blurBehavior</code> option to the context.</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;add&quot;</code> — Adds the tag to the list of tags.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;clear&quot;</code> — Clears the tags input value.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">blurBehavior</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;add&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="paste-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Paste behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#paste-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To add a tag when a arbitrary value is pasted in the input element, pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">addOnPaste</code> option.</p>
<p>When a value is pasted, the machine will:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">check if the value is a valid tag based on the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">validate</code> option</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">split the value by the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">delimiter</code> option passed</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">addOnPaste</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disable-tag-editing" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disable tag editing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disable-tag-editing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, tags can be edited by double-clicking a tag or focusing it and
pressing <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Enter</code>. To disable this behavior, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">editable: false</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">editable</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="custom-tag-delimiter" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Custom tag delimiter<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#custom-tag-delimiter"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">delimiter</code> to control how tags are created from key presses and paste.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">delimiter</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>During the lifetime of the tags input interaction, here&#x27;s a list of events we
emit:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> — invoked when the tag value changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code> — invoked when a tag has visual focus.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueInvalid</code> — invoked when the max tag count is reached or the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">validate</code>
function returns <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code>.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tagsInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;tags changed to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onHighlightChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { highlightedValue: string | null }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;highlighted tag:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">highlightedValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueInvalid</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Invalid!&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">reason</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-tag-operations" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic tag operations<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-tag-operations"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the API for imperative updates.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">addValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;React&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;React&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;TypeScript&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">clearValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// clear all</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">clearValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;React&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// clear one</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setValueAtIndex</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Vue&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">focus</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The input is focused when the user clicks on it. In this focused state, the root
and label receive <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for root focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for label focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token pseudo-class">:focus</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for input focus state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tags input is invalid by setting the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid: true</code> in the machine&#x27;s
context, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute is set on the root, input, control, and
label.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for invalid state for root */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/*  styles for invalid state for label */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/*  styles for invalid state for input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tags input is disabled by setting the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled: true</code> in the machine&#x27;s
context, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is set on the root, input, control and
label.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state for root */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state for label */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state for input */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;control&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled state for control */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>When a tag is disabled, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is set on the tag.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-preview&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for disabled tag  */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="highlighted-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a tag is highlighted via the keyboard navigation or pointer hover, a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute is set on the tag.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item-preview&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for visual focus */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="readonly-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Readonly state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#readonly-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the tags input is in its readonly state, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-readonly</code> attribute is
set on the root, label, input and control.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-readonly</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-readonly</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for readonly for input  */</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-readonly</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tags input machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; input: string; hiddenInput: string; clearBtn: string; label: string; control: string; item: (opts: ItemProps) =&gt; string; itemDeleteTrigger: (opts: ItemProps) =&gt; string; itemInput: (opts: ItemProps) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the tags input. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">maxLength</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The max length of the input.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">delimiter</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string | RegExp</code><span class="d_block">The character that serves has:
- event key to trigger the addition of a new tag
- character used to split tags when pasting into the input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em be auto-focused</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tags input should be disabled</span></li><li prose">readOnly</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tags input should be read-only</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tags input is invalid</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span boolean</code><span class="d_block">Returns a boolean that determines whether a tag can be added.

- `&quot;clear&quot;`: clear the input value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">addOnPaste</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to add a tag when you paste values into the tag input</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">max</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">number</code><span class="d_block">The max number of tags</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowOverflow</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow tags to exceed max. In this case,
we&#x27;ll attach `data-invalid` to the root</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name attribute for the input. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onPointerDownOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: PointerDownOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the pointer is pressed down outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: FocusOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when the focus is moved outside the component</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onInteractOutside</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(event: InteractOutsideEvent) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function called when an interaction happens outside the component</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

By\ndefault, tags are added when text is typed in the input field and the \u003ccode\u003eEnter\u003c/code\u003e or\n\u003ccode\u003eComma\u003c/code\u003e key is pressed. Throughout the interaction, DOM focus remains on the\ninput element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/tags-input\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"TagsInput\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTyping in the input and pressing Enter adds new tags\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eClear trigger to remove all tags\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAdd tags by pasting into the input\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDelete tags on backspace\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEdit tags after creation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eLimit the number of tags\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eNavigate tags with keyboard\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCustom validation to accept/reject tags\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the tags input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tags-input/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo set up the tags input correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"tags-input\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the tags input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as tagsInput from \"@zag-js/tags-input\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tags input package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tags-input/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eNavigating and editing tags\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the input has an empty value or the caret is at the start position, the\ntags can be selected with the left and right arrow keys. When a tag has visual\nfocus:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePress \u003ccode\u003eEnter\u003c/code\u003e or double-click the tag to edit it, then press \u003ccode\u003eEnter\u003c/code\u003e to commit\nthe change.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePressing \u003ccode\u003eDelete\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003eBackspace\u003c/code\u003e will delete the tag that has \"visual\" focus.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial tags\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo set the initial tag values, pass the \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e property in the machine's\ncontext.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"React\", \"Redux\", \"TypeScript\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled tags input\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo control the tags input programmatically, pass the \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e\nproperties to the machine function.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tags-input/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled input value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003einputValue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonInputValueChange\u003c/code\u003e when you need to control the typing\nstate separately.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  inputValue,\n  onInputValueChange(details) {\n    setInputValue(details.inputValue)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRemoving all tags\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tags input will remove all tags when the clear button is clicked. To remove\nall tags, use the provided \u003ccode\u003eclearTriggerProps\u003c/code\u003e function from the \u003ccode\u003eapi\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003e//...\n\u0026#x3C;div {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;input {...api.getInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;button {...api.getClearTriggerProps()} /\u003e\n\u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n//...\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo programmatically remove all tags, use \u003ccode\u003eapi.clearValue()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within forms\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tags input works when placed within a form and the form is submitted. We\nachieve this by:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eensuring we emit the input event as the value changes.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eadding a \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e attribute to a hidden input so the tags can be\naccessed in the \u003ccode\u003eFormData\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo get this feature working you need to pass a \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e option to the context and\nrender the hidden input with \u003ccode\u003eapi.getHiddenInputProps()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  name: \"tags\",\n  defaultValue: [\"React\", \"Redux\", \"TypeScript\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eLimiting the number of tags\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo limit the number of tags within the component, you can set the \u003ccode\u003emax\u003c/code\u003e property\nto the limit you want. The default value is \u003ccode\u003eInfinity\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the tag reaches the limit, new tags cannot be added except the\n\u003ccode\u003eallowOverflow\u003c/code\u003e option is passed to the context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-3}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  max: 10,\n  allowOverflow: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eValidating Tags\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBefore a tag is added, the machine provides a \u003ccode\u003evalidate\u003c/code\u003e function you can use to\ndetermine whether to accept or reject a tag.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote:\u003c/strong\u003e Duplicate tags are prevented by default. Set \u003ccode\u003eallowDuplicates: true\u003c/code\u003e\nto allow repeatable tags (e.g. sentence builders). Use \u003ccode\u003evalidate\u003c/code\u003e for custom\nrules like format or length.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCommon use-cases for validating tags include enforcing format, length, or\ncontent rules.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  validate(details) {\n    // Example: only allow lowercase alphabetic tags\n    return /^[a-z]+$/.test(details.inputValue)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAllow Duplicates\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, duplicate tags are prevented. For use cases like sentence builders\nor repeatable tokens, set \u003ccode\u003eallowDuplicates: true\u003c/code\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  allowDuplicates: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eBlur behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen the tags input is blurred, you can configure the action the machine should\ntake by passing the \u003ccode\u003eblurBehavior\u003c/code\u003e option to the context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\"add\"\u003c/code\u003e — Adds the tag to the list of tags.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\"clear\"\u003c/code\u003e — Clears the tags input value.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  blurBehavior: \"add\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003ePaste behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo add a tag when a arbitrary value is pasted in the input element, pass the\n\u003ccode\u003eaddOnPaste\u003c/code\u003e option.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen a value is pasted, the machine will:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003echeck if the value is a valid tag based on the \u003ccode\u003evalidate\u003c/code\u003e option\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003esplit the value by the \u003ccode\u003edelimiter\u003c/code\u003e option passed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  addOnPaste: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eDisable tag editing\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, tags can be edited by double-clicking a tag or focusing it and\npressing \u003ccode\u003eEnter\u003c/code\u003e. To disable this behavior, set \u003ccode\u003eeditable: false\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[] }\n    console.log(\"tags changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null }\n    console.log(\"highlighted tag:\", details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    console.log(\"Invalid!\", details.reason)\n a?e(a,{...n,children:e(_createMdxContent,{...n})}):_createMdxContent(n)}};function _missingMdxReference(n,e){throw new Error(\"Expected \"+(e?\"component\":\"object\")+\" `\"+n+\"` to be defined: you likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T24c2,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"Tags input renders tags inside a control, followed by an actual text input. By\ndefault, tags are added when text is typed in the input field and the `Enter` or\n`Comma` key is pressed. Throughout the interaction, DOM focus remains on the\ninput element.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/tags-input\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"TagsInput\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Typing in the input and pressing Enter adds new tags\n- Clear trigger to remove all tags\n- Add tags by pasting into the input\n- Delete tags on backspace\n- Edit tags after creation\n- Limit the number of tags\n- Navigate tags with keyboard\n- Custom validation to accept/reject tags\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the tags input package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tags-input/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the tags input correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"tags-input\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the tags input package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as tagsInput from \"@zag-js/tags-input\"\n```\n\nThe tags input package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tags-input/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Navigating and editing tags\n\nWhen the input has an empty value or the caret is at the start position, the\ntags can be selected with the left and right arrow keys. When a tag has visual\nfocus:\n\n- Press `Enter` or double-click the tag to edit it, then press `Enter` to commit\n  the change.\n- Pressing `Delete` or `Backspace` will delete the tag that has \"visual\" focus.\n\n### Setting the initial tags\n\nTo set the initial tag values, pass the `defaultValue` property in the machine's\ncontext.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"React\", \"Redux\", \"TypeScript\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled tags input\n\nTo control the tags input programmatically, pass the `value` and `onValueChange`\nproperties to the machine function.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tags-input/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Controlled input value\n\nUse `inputValue` and `onInputValueChange` when you need to control the typing\nstate separately.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  inputValue,\n  onInputValueChange(details) {\n    setInputValue(details.inputValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Removing all tags\n\nThe tags input will remove all tags when the clear button is clicked. To remove\nall tags, use the provided `clearTriggerProps` function from the `api`.\n\n```jsx {4}\n//...\n\u003cdiv {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n  \u003cinput {...api.getInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u003cbutton {...api.getClearTriggerProps()} /\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n//...\n```\n\nTo programmatically remove all tags, use `api.clearValue()`.\n\n### Usage within forms\n\nThe tags input works when placed within a form and the form is submitted. We\nachieve this by:\n\n- ensuring we emit the input event as the value changes.\n- adding a `name` and `value` attribute to a hidden input so the tags can be\n  accessed in the `FormData`.\n\nTo get this feature working you need to pass a `name` option to the context and\nrender the hidden input with `api.getHiddenInputProps()`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  name: \"tags\",\n  defaultValue: [\"React\", \"Redux\", \"TypeScript\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Limiting the number of tags\n\nTo limit the number of tags within the component, you can set the `max` property\nto the limit you want. The default value is `Infinity`.\n\nWhen the tag reaches the limit, new tags cannot be added except the\n`allowOverflow` option is passed to the context.\n\n```jsx {2-3}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  max: 10,\n  allowOverflow: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Validating Tags\n\nBefore a tag is added, the machine provides a `validate` function you can use to\ndetermine whether to accept or reject a tag.\n\n\u003e **Note:** Duplicate tags are prevented by default. Set `allowDuplicates: true`\n\u003e to allow repeatable tags (e.g. sentence builders). Use `validate` for custom\n\u003e rules like format or length.\n\nCommon use-cases for validating tags include enforcing format, length, or\ncontent rules.\n\n```jsx {2-4}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  validate(details) {\n    // Example: only allow lowercase alphabetic tags\n    return /^[a-z]+$/.test(details.inputValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Allow Duplicates\n\nBy default, duplicate tags are prevented. For use cases like sentence builders\nor repeatable tokens, set `allowDuplicates: true`:\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  allowDuplicates: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Blur behavior\n\nWhen the tags input is blurred, you can configure the action the machine should\ntake by passing the `blurBehavior` option to the context.\n\n- `\"add\"` — Adds the tag to the list of tags.\n- `\"clear\"` — Clears the tags input value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  blurBehavior: \"add\",\n})\n```\n\n### Paste behavior\n\nTo add a tag when a arbitrary value is pasted in the input element, pass the\n`addOnPaste` option.\n\nWhen a value is pasted, the machine will:\n\n- check if the value is a valid tag based on the `validate` option\n- split the value by the `delimiter` option passed\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  addOnPaste: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Disable tag editing\n\nBy default, tags can be edited by double-clicking a tag or focusing it and\npressing `Enter`. To disable this behavior, set `editable: false`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  editable: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Custom tag delimiter\n\nUse `delimiter` to control how tags are created from key presses and paste.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  delimiter: \";\",\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for events\n\nDuring the lifetime of the tags input interaction, here's a list of events we\nemit:\n\n- `onValueChange` — invoked when the tag value changes.\n- `onHighlightChange` — invoked when a tag has visual focus.\n- `onValueInvalid` — invoked when the max tag count is reached or the `validate`\n  function returns `false`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tagsInput.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[] }\n    console.log(\"tags changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string | null }\n    console.log(\"highlighted tag:\", details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    console.log(\"Invalid!\", details.reason)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic tag operations\n\nUse the API for imperative updates.\n\n```jsx\napi.addValue(\"React\")\napi.setValue([\"React\", \"TypeScript\"])\napi.clearValue() // clear all\napi.clearValue(\"React\") // clear one\napi.setValueAtIndex(0, \"Vue\")\napi.focus()\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Focused state\n\nThe input is focused when the user clicks on it. In this focused state, the root\nand label receive `data-focus`.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for root focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-focus] {\n  /* styles for label focus state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"]:focus {\n  /* styles for input focus state */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid state\n\nWhen the tags input is invalid by setting the `invalid: true` in the machine's\ncontext, the `data-invalid` attribute is set on the root, input, control, and\nlabel.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for invalid state for root */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /*  styles for invalid state for label */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-invalid] {\n  /*  styles for invalid state for input */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen the tags input is disabled by setting the `disabled: true` in the machine's\ncontext, the `data-disabled` attribute is set on the root, input, control and\nlabel.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state for root */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state for label */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state for input */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state for control */\n}\n```\n\nWhen a tag is disabled, the `data-disabled` attribute is set on the tag.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item-preview\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled tag  */\n}\n```\n\n### Highlighted state\n\nWhen a tag is highlighted via the keyboard navigation or pointer hover, a\n`data-highlighted` attribute is set on the tag.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item-preview\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for visual focus */\n}\n```\n\n### Readonly state\n\nWhen the tags input is in its readonly state, the `data-readonly` attribute is\nset on the root, label, input and control.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* styles for readonly for root */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"control\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* styles for readonly for control */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* styles for readonly for input  */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-readonly] {\n  /* styles for readonly for label */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe tags input machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"tags-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe tags input `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"tags-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"tags-input\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"tags-input\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Tags
